Youth Zone

Thunder

— Yu Xi

Saturday night, everyone went home. Those left in the dormitory were just a few of us who didn't go out much. We bought two bottles of wine, added a few dishes, and bought some beef to eat on the balcony, enjoying the cool evening breeze.

The sky was covered with dark clouds, and lightning flashed all around the horizon. The distant sound of thunder could also be faintly heard, indicating that a heavy rain was coming soon. We went inside to eat.

As expected, the rain came, and it was heavy. It beat against the roof, the balcony, and the leaves. The huge sound was like a large waterfall cascading down from the top of a mountain. And there was thunder to add to the spectacle. At first, the thunder was far away, but now it was near us, and very low, as if it were circling right on our roof. However, heavy thunderstorms are common in summer. Besides sighing that there was a lot of rain this year, we didn't pay much attention to it, until a thunderclap blew out all the lights, plunging us into terror.

At that time, the room was completely dark, but the lightning outside shone through the windows almost without interruption, illuminating the room as bright as day, seeing the wine glasses and dishes on the table, seeing the quilts and palm fans on the beds, even illuminating the foreign books on the bookshelf and the few of us standing there with frightened and dazed faces. Looking out the window, the outside world was one of thunder and lightning, with thousands of fiery serpents swirling in the sky near us. The thunder was always running around us, as if nailed to our building, determined to destroy it.

Everyone was like on the front lines, seeing those shells about to fall on them, and they were all thinking of ways to escape. Some burrowed into their blankets, while others curled up in the corners of the bed, knowing that the lightning wouldn't be so coincidental as to hit our house, but seeing the lightning and hearing the sound, they couldn't suppress their fear...

"Haha, if we get electrocuted and the whole house is destroyed, even if we who live inside try to squeeze into the cracks in the floorboards, we won't be able to escape our doomed fate. Unless we escape the dormitory. Whoever wants to live, run!"

"Running away is like seeking death. The rain outside is so heavy, and getting wet makes you more likely to be struck by lightning..."

After a moment of silence, Old Chen said urgently,

"Thank you, someone quickly close the window, glass can insulate electricity." No one except Old Jin was willing to take on this task. While closing the window, he craned his neck to look outside, saying, "That beautiful fire snake is leaping right at our eaves."

"Whoever is sitting on the iron bed, move to the floor. Iron beds easily conduct electricity." In fact, Old Xu's words already contained a joking tone, but Old Ge, who was said to be used to seeing bullets and shells, actually fell for it, making everyone laugh.

Gradually, we moved from a serious period to a playful one.

"Let's pray to God and ask him to save us."

"Oh heavens, I have never hit my parents."

"I have never bullied anyone born with eyes."

"I am loyal to my duty."

"Ah, ah, I have never thrown leftover rice grains into the urinal..."

Everyone prayed, but Old Jin was sipping wine and eating food in the dark. At that time, there was still a lot of food and wine left on the table. If he secretly ate it all by himself, wouldn't we be at a great disadvantage? So I shouted,

"Who's still drinking there at this time? How dare you? Wine easily conducts electricity!" Everyone laughed. Old Jin was a little embarrassed and also thought of a way to deal with us.

"At this time, everyone can't laugh. The God of Thunder will strike dead those who like to laugh." So, everyone spoke up and we all talked playfully, as if we had forgotten the terror of just now.

Slowly, the momentum of the thunderstorm diminished a little, and the lights came back on.

We seemed to have entered a safe period from a dangerous one. As soon as our minds were at ease, we thought of eating. Looking at the table, there was only a little bit left in the half-empty bottle of wine that was left over from just now. We still remembered that there were three packs of beef on the table, but now there wasn't a single piece left. The wine was undoubtedly eaten up by Old Jin. According to the investigation results, Old Ge hid under the covers and ate all the beef.

Distress

— De Ren

"Min has such good English and Chinese, he will definitely have a good position after graduation!" Mr. Yi said seriously, looking at the faces of many students under the podium who were listening with great interest.

The dismissal bell rang, and Mr. Yi left the classroom. Then, the students gathered to discuss what they should do after graduation.

Time passed quickly, and a class of students fortunately graduated. It has been three or four weeks now. During these three or four weeks, the graduates of course had to run around looking for places to solve their bread problem. But sadly, graduates come out year after year in large batches, but the places for them to work are not increasing in large batches. The graduates cannot find food to eat and have no way to think, so they have to return to their alma mater and ask the school authorities to think of a solution.

But sadly, it is not easy for these school authorities to barely hold on to their own places to solve their bread problems. Where do they have the spare time to manage the places for you graduates to solve your bread problems? Because it really seems like we are in a time of bread problem panic, and there are too many people who are rushing to find food as soon as they leave school.

After repeated requests from the students, the school authorities had no choice but to show a little mercy, and officially selected three or four of the more beautiful and active ones from among the many graduates to stay at the school to handle affairs. On the one hand, they were considered to have agreed to your requests, and on the other hand, they themselves also gained an advantage, because they could hire them with meager salaries. Anyway, they voluntarily asked to come, and they are recent graduates with insufficient experience, humble food seekers.

A few students with good memories saw that Min was not selected to handle affairs in the school and seized on Mr. Yi's saying, "Min has such good English and Chinese, he will definitely have a good position after graduation," and asked Mr. Yi. Mr. Yi kindly deflected the reply. In fact, these students who asked Mr. Yi were too ignorant. How could they be so rude as to not understand the original intention of Mr. Yi's words? If they thought carefully, they could immediately understand that Mr. Yi's words were meant to make the students study diligently, and that he himself was not responsible for saying these words.

As a result, the school still used those few beautiful and active ones. The other students, even the one Mr. Yi had said "will have a good position," were still not selected. They withdrew from the school and had no choice but to sit at home listlessly, bitterly resenting the difficulty of finding food to eat in society.

Youth Garden Guidelines

(1) The text should be related to discussions of youth issues, domestic and foreign school or student news, essays, descriptions of school life, notes, etc. The style is not limited.

(2) Pictures should be limited to those related to youth issues.

(3) Photos of youth life (such as sports, travel, travelogues, drama performances, lectures, gatherings, exhibitions, various competitions, etc.), school news, and youth movements are eligible, regardless of whether they are individuals or groups. Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(5) Write manuscripts horizontally and do not write sloppily. Western text should be omitted where possible. If it is unavoidable to cite the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

Regardless of whether the submitted manuscripts are published or not, they will not be returned. If they need to be returned,
